#############################################
# Innovation policies
#############################################
#Plutocracy : Idea cost (Les Lumières)
#Divine : Missionary strenght (new method of indoctrination)
#Aristocracy : Institution cost (fewer people need to know)
#Horde : Institution spread (Ancestor teaching, in the end it's still ponies teaching)
#Colonial Empire : Settler chance / innovativness gain
#Espionnage : Institution spread + / Tech cost -  / Innovativness gain + (Tech Spy)
#Diplomatic : Diplomatice relation / War exaustion -
#Influence : Vassal force limit contribution / Prestige decay
#Trade : Trade steering ++ (Schumptérian Buisness)
#Exploration : Colonial Range +++ (Everyone must do like Alariandel)
#Maritime : Ship durability /  innovativness gain
#Assimilation : diplo tech cost ( idea of the other)
#Nationalism : mil tech cost ( idea of our people)
#Society : adm tech cost (innovation of a new society)
#propaganda : Power Projection From Insult ++ (Invention of social media increase the toxicity)
#Imperialist ambition : Military tech cost (Army investment)
#Imperialism : Military tech cost (Army investment)
#High Seas : Flagship Durability + / Ship durability
#Amphibious Ideas : Disembarkement Speed/ Transport Attrition (New landing method)
#Magocratic : magical study experience ( library of wisdom)
#Monstruous : Razing gain ++
#Empire of Anbennar Ideas : Reson to Elect ( elect the smart guy)
#Artificery : Artificery Privilege Slot (Technological advantage)
#War Production : Artillery Cost, army maintenance ( lighter steel for canon)
#Shock : Shock damage ++ (Raming With High speed)
#Fire : Artillery Available Vs Fort (Grosse Bertha)
#Offensive : Max Land Leader Maneuvre (Eren jägeeeeeer tatakae policy)
#Defensive : shock damage recieve (square formation)
#Quality : Military Tactics (Minimal) (inovation from officer school)
#Quantity : reform progress growth ++ (emergence of idea in the mass)
#Strategic Ideas : Artillery Available Vs Fort(Stacked fire power against fort)
#Serpentspine : Construction Time(The best of drills)
#Legionary ideas : Land attrition - (Survive under the sun)
#General Staff Ideas : Yearly army tradition decay (Sparking genius general)
#Standing Army : Artificers capacity + /Special Unit Force Limit minimal
#Heroism : idea cost / mercenary maintenace
#Conscription : Innovativeness Gain / manpower recovery
#Weapon Quality : military tech cost / infantry combat ability
#Forteress :  Hostile Attrition ++ (Feu grégeois)
#Militarism  : Infantry combat ability ++ (Better guns for our units)

#############################################
# Economic policies
#############################################
#Plutocracy : Inflation + Tax Modifier +++ (The true BCE experience)
#Divine : Tolerance of Heathen - Tax Modifier +++ (For our poor heathens of course)
#Aristocracy : Global Unrest +2 Tax Modifier +++ (What? I dont hear you)
#Horde : cavalry cost - (Negotiation around the Wheat for ponies)
#Colonial Empire : Treasure Fleet Income ++ /  inflation decrease (Make bigger boats to carry all that stuff v2)
#Espionnage : Favor Growth increase (If we can't get it legaly, we will blackmail them to pay us)
#Diplomatic : Trade Transfer Acceptance (The new deal, Absolutely not a scam I promise)
#Influence : Vassal income +++ (Suck them dry, we need more taxes)
#Trade : Trade efficiency ++
#Exploration : Treasure Fleet Income ++ / Monthly inflation decrease (Make bigger boats to carry all that stuff!)
#Maritime : Trade Ship Power / Cost to promote mercantilism (The golden flow of commerce)
#Assimilation : Merchant trade power ++ (Interacial trade customs)
#Nationalism : production efficiency ++/ unrest + (Immigrants Go to work!)
#Society : Tax +++ (Tax meta is the correct Meta)
#propaganda : War Taxes Cost -50%
#Imperialist ambition : Interest / inflation reduction cost (The path of conquest, but at a cheeper price)
#Imperialism : Tax +++ / Vassal income (Tax the shit out of them!)
#High Seas : trade ship power ++ (The money path is via the sea)
#Amphibious Ideas : Embargo Efficiency ++ / Blockade impact on siege /Blockade Efficiency (The Amphibious warfare)
#Magocratic : Gold depletion chance 50% (Magical gold veins)
#Monstruous : Available loot / Razing gain / Privateer Efficiency (The way of the Monsters)
#Empire of Anbennar Ideas : Tax +++ / Empire tax +++ (Apoint new taxes for the glorious empror)
#Artificery : special unit cost / Tax +
#War Production : War taxes -50% (War ready economy)
#Shock : Cavalry cost - / Tax
#Fire : Military advisor cost / Construction cost
#Offensive : Marchant Trade Power (Agressive Merchant Economic tactic)
#Defensive : Shock damage recived / Fire damage recived (Cheeper metal deals)
#Quality : Inflation reduction modifier (Better minting policies)
#Quantity : Tax ++++ / Inflation gain modifier + (Far too much taxes)
#Strategic Ideas : War taxes -50% (War economy fueled)
#Serpentspine : Construction cost / fort maintenance (Surface holds pride)
#Legionary ideas : Production efficiency + / Yearly prestige (Silk market of bulwar)
#General Staff Ideas : Free Leader ++ / Advisor cost -
#Standing Army : Drill gain  ++ / Drill decay - (Follow an online formation it's cheeper and faster they say)
#Heroism : Mercenary maintenance - / Mercenary cost
#Conscription : Infantry cost / Cavalry cost / Artillery cost
#Weapon Quality : Good produced modifier ++ (Produce more with low space)
#Forteress :  Fort maintenance / Fort maintenance bordering rivals (And Mexicans are gonna pay for it)
#Militarism  : Infantry cost - - (Sustained payroll)

#############################################
# Expansion policies
#############################################
#Plutocracy : settler chance (homme libre)
#Divine : global settler increase (Ryōiki Tenkai)
#Aristocracy : settler chance (King's oversea expedition subside)
#Horde : global settler increase (steps suck mate)
#Colonial Empire : Colonist ++ (The True way of expansion)
#Espionnage : Cost to fabricate claim
#Diplomatic : Agressive expansion impact
#Influence : Center of trade upgrade / Liberty desire in subject
#Trade : Trade power from dev (Upgrade exisitng trade companies)
#Exploration : Colonist +1 / Settler chance
#Maritime : colonial range / Trade range
#Assimilation : native assimilation / native uprising chance
#Nationalism : native uprising chance /expel minorities cost
#Society : marchant +1 / settler increase
#propaganda : setller chance/ Agressive expansion impact (go in the colony for your country
#Imperialist ambition : Vassalisation acceptance
#Imperialism : Liberty desire from Dev of subject
#High Seas : trade steering / Settler increase
#Amphibious Ideas : Claim oversee (Your coast can be ours in instant)
#Magocratic : Good produced modifier ++ (Duplication of pumkins by magic)
#Monstruous : Agressive expansion impact
#Empire of Anbennar Ideas : colony cost ( empire of anbennar financial support to expand)
#Artificery : Special Unit Force Limit + (Artificier of aelantir)
#War Production : production / settler increase
#Shock : Agressive expansion impact / Shock damage
#Fire : Agressive expansion impact  / Fire damage 
#Offensive : colonist + 1 / free land leader  +1
#Defensive : native uprising chance (Better than chevaux de frise to protect our colony)
#Quality : Settler chance (Better equipment for settlers)
#Quantity : Settler increase (Mass colonialism)
#Strategic Ideas : colony cost (better managment of expansion ressource)
#Serpentspine : Settler chance (Better caverns)
#Legionary ideas : Settler increase / Infantry combat ability
#General Staff Ideas : land leader fire ( the gouvernor)
#Standing Army : dicipline / settler increase (diciplined expansionnist)
#Heroism : mercennary cost / native assimilation ( native mercenary)
#Conscription : colony cost (The australian experience)
#Weapon Quality : production efficiency / regiment cost
#Forteress :  Construction cost / core creation cost
#Militarism  : Infantry combat ability / Native assimilation

    monarch_power = DIP

    potential = {
        has_idea_group = expansion_ideas

    allow = {
        full_idea_group = expansion_ideas
        full_idea_group = plutocracy_ideas
    }

    colonist_placement_chance = 0.05

    ai_will_do = {
        factor = 1
    }
}

#Nationalism : Culture conversion cost
#Society : reform progress ++
#propaganda : Core creation cost
#Imperialist ambition : Core creation cost
#Imperialism : State governing cost / State governing capacity
#High Seas : Privateer Efficiency (High end corsairs)
#Amphibious Ideas : Privateer Efficiency (Mandate for costal assault)
#Magocratic : Monthly devastation (Safe regrowth act, equivalent à la décision des mages pour faire pousser des plantes)

#Defensive : fort defence/ Hostile attrition
#Quality : army trad/ yearly professionalism
#Quantity : drill gain / drill decay
#Strategic Ideas : Cost to fabricate claim
#Serpentspine : Core creation cost / Build speed
#Legionary ideas : Governement capacity / Income from Vassal
#General Staff Ideas : Leader without upkeep / Advisor cost / Possible advisor
#Standing Army : Special Unit Force Limit
#Heroism : allow mercenaries to split (individual contracts)
#Conscription : Force limit/ manpower
#Weapon Quality : production efficiency / infantry combat  ability
#Forteress :  fort defence / yearly tax income
#Militarism  : Magician equilibrium / Core creation cost (Magical fake claims for adminitrative purpose)

#############################################
# Tolerance policies
#############################################
#Plutocracy : Republican tradition 
#Divine : Devotion
#Aristocracy : Legitimacy / Meritocracy
#Horde : Horde unity
#Colonial Empire : Liberty Desire on Other Continent (Down the liberty desire only for colonies)
#Espionnage : Rebel support efficiency +++ (VIVA LA REVOLUTIONNNNN!) / Diplomatic impact on covert operation
#Diplomatic : Improve Relations  /Diplomatic Reputation
#Influence : Liberty desire of subject
#Trade : Caravan Power/ Improve Relations Modifier (Fair Trade, Woke Edition)
#Exploration : Native Assimilation, Improve Relations (Diversity Discoverers)
#Maritime : Privateer Efficiency / Naval tradition ( Woke Waves)
#Assimilation : merc_independent_from_trade_range
#Nationalism : Unrest + / Diplomatic rep - (Go woke go broke)
#Society : Global Unrest/ Stability Cost Modifier (Safe space for All)
#propaganda : Rebel support efficiency +++ (VIVA LA REVOLUTIONNNNN!)
#Imperialist ambition : Years of Separatism - - - (Force integration of newly aquired land)
#Imperialism : Harsh treatment cost - (Force suppression of Newly aquired land)
#High Seas : Naval force limit / Cuture slot
#Amphibious Ideas : Marines force limit / Cuture slot
#Magocratic : Artificiary capacity (Cohexistance Act)
#Monstruous : Diplomatic reputation +++ (Qui prendrait ça??)
#Empire of Anbennar Ideas : Resistance to reform / Tolerance of heretics
#Artificery : Mage influence / Mage loyality equilibrium (Cohexistance Act)
#War Production : Global Regiment Cost / Artillery Cost ( Guns for All, DEI quota)
#Shock : Cav/Inf Ratio (Nous ne faisons qu'un avec les poney! Sus...)
#Fire : Fire Damage/Warscore Cost vs Other Religion(Burning with Acceptance.Wait ,they claim to be tolerant but use the methods of those they criticize)
#Offensive : Discipline/ Siege ability (Tolerance Through Superior Firepower)
#Defensive : religious unity / unrest + ( defend minority (eww))
#Quality : Inf combat / cav combat / artillery combat (Equally Exceptional)
#Quantity : MP / FL ( One BIg Happy Army)
#Strategic Ideas : Unrest + (Not every dwarves is ovdal lodhum)
#Serpentspine : Unrest - - (The teaching of unity under the scorching sun)
#Legionary ideas : Leader Cost / Land Leader Manneuvre ( Diversity in Command)
#General Staff Ideas : land leader fire ( the gouvernor)
#Standing Army : Special Unit Force Limit /Land Maintenance Modifier (Integration of Special Army)
#Heroism : Mercenary Discipline /Tolerance of Heathens(Inclusive Chivalry)
#Conscription : Global Manpower Modifier/ Reinforce Speed( Drafting Diversity) 
#Weapon Quality : Infantry Fire / Cavalry Shock ( Equi-table Firepower)
#Forteress : Religious unity / Garrison size/ Global garrison growth
#Militarism  : national unrest / Morale or armies

#############################################
# Religious policies
#############################################
#jurispudence : War cost against other religions
#Plutocracy : Religious Unity
#Divine : No religious penalty (Find god, God is everything)
#Aristocracy : Missionary Strengh/ Missionary Cost
#Horde : Years of separatism (unity under religion)
#Colonial Empire : Global Missionary Strength/ Settler Chance (Cross and Crown)
#Espionnage : Spy Network / War Cost vs Other Religion ( Holy Shadow)
#Diplomatic : Relation bonus for same religion
#Influence : Enforce religion Cost
#Trade : Marchant / trade Efficiency (FaithFull Marachant)
#Exploration : Missionary Stenght / Settler Increase/ Native Assimilation (Missionaries Aboard)
#Maritime : Naval Tradition from Trade/Missionary Strenght (Holy fleet)
#Assimilation : No Penalty of other religions (Complete secularism)
#Nationalism : Missionary strenght / Prestige from conversion (Purge the heretics)
#Society : Missionary Maintenace /Stability Cost Modifier (FaithFull Fondation)
#propaganda : Yearly legetimacy / Missionary Strengh (The Holy Word Machine)
#Imperialist ambition : War cost against other religions
#Imperialism : Religious unity ++
#High Seas : missionary maintenance / ship cost
#Amphibious Ideas : missionary maintenance / Marines force limit
#Magocratic : Clergy privilege slot /Loyauty Mage / Influance Mage (Clerics of the Arcane)
#Monstruous : Shock Damage/ Clergy Influance - (Sanctified Beasts)
#Empire of Anbennar Ideas : Resistance to reform / Missionary strenght Vs heretics / Cost to enact holy orders
#Artificery : Artillerie Fire ( canon of Lavalette)
#War Production : Artilerry cost / artilerry fire ( Orgue canon, Forged by Faith)
#Shock : Shock damage (A man with an horse is physicaly but also spiritually more powerful than an footmen)
#Fire : Fire Damage / Missionary Strengh/ warcost vs other Religion( Cleansing Flames)
#Offensive : War cost against other religions
#Defensive : global heretic missionary strength / tolerence of true faith (defend our country againts those herticts)
#Quality : Discipline / Inf comnat (Divine Perfection)
#Quantity : Manpower in true faith province
#Strategic Ideas : Clergy privilege slot/ Army Tradition From Battle(Holy Stratagems)
#Serpentspine : Missionary +1 (Proselytism in the serpentspine)
#Legionary ideas : Missionary strenght ++ (The removal of Sun heresy)
#General Staff Ideas : Leader Land Fire/Army Morale Recovery Speed(Divine GeneralShip)
#Standing Army : Army Morale / Land Maintenance (Holy Host)
#Heroism : Global Missionary Strength/ Mercenary Cost (Crusaders for Hire)
#Conscription : Manpower in true faith province
#Weapon Quality : Land fire Damage (Blessed Steel)
#Forteress :  Garrison damage (Our faith is strong)
#Militarism  : Shock infantry (flat minimal) (Holy bayonet)

# Elven Supremacy policies
#############################################
#health : Avg monarch livespawn + (will you die one day ?)
#Plutocracy : random bonus candidate (plus vieux = plus intelligent)
#Divine : Devotion / Religious power / Missonary stenght (Elven know only one faith)
#Aristocracy : Legitimacy / Gouvernment capacity (The Rightful Heir of the Mythical elven empire)
#Horde : Detruire toute la qualité elfe, Donner la qualité centaure (wtf mate??)
#Colonial Empire : Supression du débuff elf de la colonisation
#Espionnage : Foreign spy detection / Support rebel efficiency ++ (Doctrine Monroe for south aelantir)
#Diplomatic : Power Projection From Insult +++ (We hate you, you are not an elf)
#Influence : Diplomatic Relations (More minions for the elven pride)
#Trade : Trade ship power (Rule Aelnar)
#Exploration : Settler increase ++ (Make Aelnar Great Again)
#Maritime : Ship durability (The real invincible Armada)
#Assimilation :  Unrest + (What did you expect?)
#Nationalism : Culture convert cost  - - - / Max promoted culture - - - (Gas Gas GAAAS Initial D reference of course)
#Society : Culture convert cost (The best society is an elven society)
#propaganda : harsh treatment cost - - -/ Max absolutism (HAIL ELVEN SUPREMACY)
#Imperialist ambition : Diplomatic reputation / prestige (Elven "courtoisy")
#Imperialism : Rebel suppression efficiency( sucombe au reich)
#High Seas : Combat bonus of owned coast (Mare Nostrum)
#Amphibious Ideas : Marines force limit (Manpower is useless anyway)
#Magocratic : all power cost (magical elf is just better)
#Monstruous :  Détruire la qualité elfe, Donner la qualité ruinborn AUGMENTE (Disaster Class)
#Empire of Anbennar Ideas : Reson to elect (Ibevar you got this!)
#Artificery : Special Unit Force Limit (The Special Soldier Division :Wink Wink:)
#War Production : War exaustion + / Production efficiency (Macron Law)
#Shock : Cavalry combat ability + (Horse is the only worthy comanions of elves)
#Fire :  Land fire damage small (The mithical caber toss of elven)
#Offensive : Agressive expansion impact (Elvens claim the world)
#Defensive : Fort Maintenance on border with rival (Leibensrüm) 
#Quality : Discipline ++ / Manpower recovery speed - (Elven quality)
#Quantity :  Heir chance / Manpower recovery speed (We learn the importance of reproducing)
#Strategic Ideas : Agressive expansion impact, Movement Speed (Blitz Kreig Tactics)
#Serpentspine : Detruire toute la qualité Elfe, Donner la qualitée naine (Where are you going elf? Are you lost?)
#Legionary ideas : Reduce morale damage taken by reserves (Phoenix empire never surrender!)
#General Staff Ideas : Drill lost / Drill gain modifier (Train Harder Better Faster Stronger)
#Standing Army :  Special Unit Force Limit (designed by Hugo boss)
#Heroism :  Mercenary discipline (Train them harder than elves!)
#Conscription :  National force limit (More enlisted elves)
#Weapon Quality :  Fire damage + (Bow IS better than guns, if used by an elf)
#Forteress :  Garrison damage (THIS IS OUR FOREST!)
#Militarism  : Infantry combat ability + (Phoenix experience)

#############################################
# Jurisprudence policies
#############################################
#Plutocracy : change national focus - (Quicker reaction of the government)
#Divine : change national focus - (Quicker reaction of the government)
#Aristocracy : change national focus - (Quicker reaction of the government)
#Horde : change national focus - (Quicker reaction of the government)
#Colonial Empire : Liberty Desire on Other Continent (Down the liberty desire only for colonies)
#Espionnage : Enemy core creation cost on us
#Diplomatic : Agressive expansion impact - - (Legitimate our wars)
#Influence : Liberty desire of subject
#Trade : Cost to justify a trade conflict / Trade ship power / Privateer efficiency (The agressive market knowledge)
#Exploration : Unjustified demand / Cost to fabricate a claim (Claiming Native territory with ease)
#Maritime : Unjustified demand / Navy tradition
#Assimilation : Power Projection From Insult (Cancel culture generalized)
#Nationalism : Faster explusion / Faster extermination (Purge by law)OR cultur conversion time et cost
#Society : Stab hit form declaring a war (L'Etat de droit de mettre ma main dans ta gueule)
#propaganda : Covert action relation impact (Right to spy your neighbor)
#Imperialist ambition : Agressive expansion impact (Justified conquest)
#Imperialism : Liberty desire of subject
#High Seas : Privateer efficiency (Lettres de marque)
#Amphibious Ideas : Privateer efficiency (Lettres de marque)
#Magocratic : Diplomatic reputation +2 (Deregulation of magic is now legal)
#Monstruous : Unjustified demand / Horde unity(Conqueror keepers)
#Empire of Anbennar Ideas : Unjustified demand / Improve relation (Legal way of blobing the empire)
#Artificery : Military Technology Cost- (Artificier law)
#War Production : Enemy core creation cost on us (Protecting our Heart land from enemy takeover)
#Shock : Good produced +0,25 (Legal Slave contract)
#Fire :  Artillery available VS fort 
#Offensive : Unjustified demand / land attrition
#Defensive : enemy core creation on us (Failed referundum for rattachement)
#Quality : Core creation cost / Discipline
#Quantity :  Idea cost / Land force limit
#Strategic Ideas : allow_free_estate_privilege_revocation (Complete authority of the state)
#Serpentspine : Construction time (Constrain Dwarvens guilds)
#Legionary ideas : Liberty desire on same continent - - / Diplomatic Annexation Cost - (Unification of Bulwar abided by Law)
#General Staff Ideas : Yearly corruption / Army tradition decay (Alexander strategic)
#Standing Army :  Discipline / Yearly corruption (Men of integrity in the ranks)
#Heroism : Mercenary Maintenance Modifier/Harsh Treatment Cost (Guardians of Justice)
#Conscription : Naional Manpower increase (Lower the age of conscription)
#Weapon Quality :  Military technlology cost (Reaserch of beter equiipment)
#Forteress : Fort bordering rival MAX / Garrison size  (Justified border)
#Militarism  : Yearly corruption / Moral of armies

#Centralisation : Centralize state cost
#Decentralisation : Trade Company Invesment Cost 
#infrastructures : upgrade cost of trade center (we need more trade)
#Colonial Empire : Liberty Desire on Other Continent (Sisters republics)
#Espionnage : rebel support efficiency / spy network construction (Levy the horde)
#Diplomatic : Revolution zeal ++ / Diplomat +1 / Loyalty of burghers (Lorentish revolution)
#Influence : Diplomatic relation/ republican tradition
#Trade : Merchant +1 (La serenissima)
#Exploration : Native uprising chance / republican tradition (Spreading democracy to natives)
#Maritime : Galley combat ability +++ (Venice Arsenal)
#Assimilation : Max promoted culture +++ / Culture integration cost + (Lorent Melting pot)
#Nationalism : Culture conversion cost (Intern Colonisation)
#Society : Trade efficiency (Trade policies enhanced)
#propaganda : Election lenght + / Random candidat bonus +1 (A true model of democracy)
#Imperialist ambition : Dev cost (Marshall Plan)
#Imperialism : Prod efficiency (Five year plan)
#High Seas :trade power in fleet modifier( comercial trade fleet)
#Amphibious Ideas : privateering efficiency in fleet modifier ( prirates fleet)
#Magocratic : Republican tradition (Master of illusion in a Democracy) (Macronisme?)
#Monstruous : Election term - / Reelection cost - (Rule by chaos)
#Empire of Anbennar Ideas : Trade steering / Merchant trade power (The richies of Anbennar)
#Artificery :Special Unit Force Limite(Republican Elite Guard)
#War Production : Production efficiency / Regiment cost
#Shock : Shock damage recived / Republican tradition
#Fire :  Backrow artillery damage (zeppelin fire)
#Offensive : Recruitment general cost (Outcast officers)
#Defensive : Garrison size (Guardian of the republic)
#Quality : Infantry combat ability
#Quantity :  Force limit (Wave of peasant)
#Strategic Ideas :Movement speed / Supply limit (Zeplin auxiliaries)
#Serpentspine : Construction cost / construction speed (Council of Dwarven deepeners)
#Legionary ideas : Discipline + (The Human rule)
#General Staff Ideas : Leader cost (More gerenals for duty)
#Standing Army :  Regiment drill loss / Discipline minimal
#Heroism : Aventurer privilege slot / Republican tradition 
#Conscription : Manpower recovery speed (Uncle sam Recruitment)
#Weapon Quality :  Maintenance of army / Good produced modifier (Potato army weponized)
#Forteress : Garrison size (Unbreakable forteress of the republic)
#Militarism  : Diplo relation / Shock damage

#############################################
# Theocracy policies
#############################################
#State administration : Missionary maintenance / Gouvernment capacity (état de droit divin)
#Centralism : National tax modifier
#Decentralism : True Faith Tolerence
#Infrastructure : National Tax (Increased Religious thite)
#Colonial Empire : Treasure Fleet Income +++ (Templar gold)
#Espionnage : Diplomat +1 / Spy network construction ++ (Secrets of the holy orders)
#Diplomatic : Missionary +1 / Devotion / Diplomatic reputation / loyalty of religious / Loyalty of Magicians / Cost to apoint Verdicals (Holy mandate)
#Influence : Cost to enforce religion - - / relation with coutry with the same religion
#Trade : Merchant trade power / Missionary strenght (Emissary of the true faith)
#Exploration : Native Assimilation (Inquisition Orders)
#Maritime : Piracy efficiency / Available loot (Malta order)
#Assimilation : Heathen tolerance + / Heretical tolerance + (New Dhimi Deal)
#Nationalism : Tolerance of true faith ++/ Heathen tolerance - / Heretical tolerance - (God know his mens)
#Society : Missionary strenght (Priesthood society)
#propaganda : Devotion / Tolerance of true faith (LFI cult of personality)
#Imperialist ambition : Cost of war against othe religion (Jihad policie)
#Imperialism : Religious unity / Missionary stenght (Dhimi integration)
#High Seas : cannons for hunting pirates in fleet (divine fire on criminal)
#Amphibious Ideas : cannons for hunting pirates in fleet (divine fire on criminal)
#Magocratic : Diplo rep + / Diplo rep ++++ if lich / Diplo relation +1 (The quintescence of lichdom)
#Monstruous : Agressive expansion impact / Shock damage ++ (Netherworld Quality)
#Empire of Anbennar Ideas :Diplomat +1/ Improve relation ++ (Divine Emissaries)
#Artificery : Special unit force Limit (Rubyhold Elite guard)
#War Production : Production efficiency / Recruitment time (Light a candle for the machines)
#Shock : Shock damage minimal (Gandalf Ent charge)
#Fire :  Land fire (Holy fire of homebrew)
#Offensive : Warscore cost against other religion
#Defensive : Garrison damage (Fremen assault)
#Quality : Land Morale (Flagelant army)
#Quantity :  Force limit (Pierre l'hermit crusaders)
#Strategic Ideas : Attrition for enemies (the 7 plagues of the khet)
#Serpentspine : Warscore cost against other religion (Fight for the rocks)
#Legionary ideas : Moral damage taken by reserves - (Jaher Light guide us all)
#General Staff Ideas : Leader cost (More gerenals for duty)
#Standing Army :  Yearly professionalism / Discipline minimal
#Heroism : Mercenary Discipline/Yearly Devotion (Divine Crusaders/Paladin)
#Conscription : Moral revovery speed / Fort defence ( Scutum Dei)
#Weapon Quality :  Morale damage / Morale damage recived (Light a candle for the Weapons)
#Forteress : Attrition for enemies (Holy light for every forteress)
#Militarism  : Devotion / Mage equilibrium

#############################################
# Aristocracy policies
#############################################
#State administration :Gouvernment capacity / Legitimacy
#Centralism :Diplo annexion cost
#Decentralism : Liberty desire in subject
#Infrastructure : Great project cost - (Wonder worthy of the royalty)
#Colonial Empire : Global tariffs ++ (Royal tariffs)
#Espionnage : Diplomat +1 / Foreign spy detection ++ (Court intrigue)
#Diplomatic : Diplomat +1 / Legitimacy / Meritocracy / Loyalty of nobles (Solar phoenix King)
#Influence : Year of personal union integration (One familiy multiple thrones)
#Trade : Merchant +1 (Recruit more merchant)
#Exploration : Expulsion of minorities cost / Settler increase (Penal colonies)
#Maritime : cannons_for_hunting_pirates_in_fleet (Anti piracy decree)
#Assimilation : Max promoted culture (The jaad experience)
#Nationalism : Culture conversion cost (Bismark ?)
#Society : Tax +++ (Royal tax)
#propaganda : Unrest - (One to rule them all)
#Imperialist ambition : Vassalisation acceptance (Pupet master)
#Imperialism : Diplomatic Annexation Cost(Rooting the almighty power)
#High Seas :barrage cost in fleet modifier ( competente admiral)
#Amphibious Ideas : barrage cost in fleet modifier ( competente admiral)
#Magocratic : Mage equilibrium / Learning magic faster (Taste of magic)
#Monstruous : Cavalry combat ability / Infantry combat ability (Royal guard reinforced)
#Empire of Anbennar Ideas :Reason to elect / Authority growth (L'empreur c'est moi)
#Artificery :Special unit force Limit (Elites of the crown)
#War Production : Artificery privilege slot
#Shock : Cavalry combat ability (Powerful knight)
#Fire :  Land leader fire / Amiral leader fire (Actually good Aristocrat generals)
#Offensive : Unjustified demand
#Defensive : Garrison size (Sardokar regiment)
#Quality : Cav/Inf ratio (Bretonia will vanquish)
#Quantity :  Special Unit Force Limit (Ahati Dragon guard)
#Strategic Ideas :Artillery available VS fort (Fraking cannon)
#Serpentspine : Construction cost / Construction speed (There can only be one king under the moutain)
#Legionary ideas : Monarch military power / prestige from land battle (Tu quoque heres es Jaher)
#General Staff Ideas : Leader cost (More gerenals for duty)
#Standing Army :  Army drill gain modifier / Discipline minimal
#Heroism : Mercenary discipline / Prestige from battle (White falcon Army)
#Conscription : Manpower recovery speed  (indelningsverket)
#Weapon Quality :  Discipline (Ceremonial weapons)
#Forteress : Garrison damage (Chivalry sortie)
#Militarism  : Cav/Inf ratio  (Knights Cohorte tactics)

#############################################
# Horde policies
#############################################
#State administration :Horde unity / Gouvernment capacity
#Centralism :Change capital cost
#Decentralism :Agressive expansion impact
#Infrastructure :cavalry cost - (more stable for ponies)
#Colonial Empire :Settler chance - / Piracy efficiency ++ (Steal the treasure fleet)
#Espionnage : Enemy core creation cost on us / Foreign spy detection (Possession of the horde can't be possession of anyone else)
#Diplomatic : Diplomat +1 / Available loot ++ / Razing gain / horde unity  (Clan council)
#Influence : Relation slot (More tributaries)
#Trade : Caravan power (Cantaury couriers)
#Exploration : Colonial range ++ (Land we've never seen befoe)
#Maritime : Piracy efficiency / Available loot (Barbary coast pack)
#Assimilation : Cav/Inf ratio (Assimilation of the riding doctrine (illusion of choice))
#Nationalism : Cav/Inf ratio (We steal thier horses anyway (illusion of choice))
#Society : Raze power gain (Conquest of foreign land)
#propaganda : Sensibility to Agressive expansion impact (Je sais pas si c'est possible) (Winter is never comming TKT frère) OR AE genre agressive expension IMPACT
#Imperialist ambition : Agressive expansion impact (the unstoppable Steamroller)
#Imperialism : Years of separatism (Break thier mind to surrender)
#High Seas : movement speed in fleet modifier (ponies have 4 legs to pedal) 
#Amphibious Ideas : movement speed in fleet modifier (ponies have 4 legs to pedal) 
#Magocratic : Movment speed (Magical hoofs to speed up)
#Monstruous : Cav/Inf ratio / Cav combat ability (Centaur supremacy)
#Empire of Anbennar Ideas : Diplo rep -4 (What are you doing here? World conquest?)
#Artificery : Cavalry fire Minimal (Centaur tank Issou)
#War Production : Production efficiency / Cavalry cost (Adapted machines for the centaurs)
#Shock : Cavalry flanking ability (Outsmart Manoeuver)
#Fire :  Artillery shock Minimal (Centaur tank Issou)
#Offensive : Cavalry combat ability
#Defensive : Attrition for enemies (Hoof-ed Earth) (Terre sabot-é)
#Quality : Shock damage
#Quantity :  Force limit (Singe-ed)
#Strategic Ideas :Tactics + Minimal (Plagued body are thrown on our enemies)
#Serpentspine : Delete Centaur military, Give Dwarven military (Wtf are you doing here?)
#Legionary ideas : Discipline + (Rival worthy of bulwar apear)
#General Staff Ideas : Recruitment general cost / Army tradition (More land to aquire, need more generals)
#Standing Army :  Fire damage recived - / Discipline minimal(Plated horses)
#Heroism : Mercenary discipline (There is man amongst us now)
#Conscription : Force limit modifier / Supply limit (Ten thousand men army)
#Weapon Quality :  Cavalry combat ability ++ (Al-Battar)
#Forteress : Siege ability + (We know how it's build, We know how to destroy it)
#Militarism  : Shock damage + (New shock tactics learned)

# State administration policies
#############################################
#Colonial Empire : Liberty Desire on Other Continent (Down the liberty desire only for colonies)
#Espionnage : Reform progress growth / Institution spread (Wispering new ideas)
#Diplomatic : all estate loyalty equilibrium (All unemployed to the adminitration)
#Influence : Diplomatique relation slot ++ (Better management of vassals)
#Trade : Caravan power ++ (More power from the land we own)
#Exploration : Government capacity (Exile contract for bureaucrats)
#Maritime : Institution spread + (Secured maritime lanes of knowledge)
#Assimilation : Max promoted culture + / Cost to promote culture - (Multi culturalism experience)
#Nationalism : Cost of expulsion of minorities / culture conversion cost (Purging the spawn)
#Society : Reform progress ++ (Paper scraper enhance the state innovation)
#propaganda : Autonomy change cooldown - (Administration handles campaigns more seriously)
#Imperialist ambition : Administrative efficiency + (Growing exponentially)
#Imperialism : Gouvernment capacity +++ (Better gestion of the territory)
#High Seas : Gouvernment capacity / Naval force limit
#Amphibious Ideas : State governing cost / Marines force limit
#Magocratic : Administrative efficiency (Magician aid for the paperwork)
#Monstruous : Reform progess +30% (Catching up the reform)
#Empire of Anbennar Ideas :Reform progress growth ++ (Ebullition of the new things)
#Artificery :All Estate loyalty equilibrium
#War Production : centralize_state_cost (Nationalisation contract of the factories)
#Shock : Shock damage / Reform progress growth
#Fire :  Fire damage / Autonomy change cooldown
#Offensive : Core Creation Cost - (Assimilation of recent conquest)
#Defensive : yearly corruption/ Morale of armies
#Quality : Discipline minimal / Reform progress Growth
#Quantity :  Force limit / Gouvernment capacity
#Strategic Ideas :All estates loyalty equilibrium  (Absolutism impact of privilieges) (Court magnigance)
#Serpentspine : Refrom progress modifier ++
#Legionary ideas : Gouvernment capacity modifier ++ (Cradle of the phoenix empire)
#General Staff Ideas : Army Professionalism / Corruption - (Leader exeptional payroll)
#Standing Army :  Army tradition decay / Reform progress growth(Civil servant army)
#Heroism : Mercenary discipline minimal / Corruption - (The independant audit of the army)
#Conscription : State mainteance / Reform progress growth (Even more Civil Servant)
#Weapon Quality :  regiment cost / Production efficiency (Military purchase from the state)
#Forteress : State maintenance / Fort defence
#Militarism  : State maintenance / Infantry combat ability

# centralism policies

#Colonial Empire :Administrative Efficiency/ Liberty From subject desire (The Sun Never Sets)
#Espionnage : Spy Network / Unrest / diplomats (Spider's Web Network)
#Diplomatic : Diplomatic Reputation / Improve Relation/ Envoy Travel Time (Iron Quill)
#Influence : unrest - -
#Trade : Trade efficiency / caravan power 
#Exploration : core creation cost
#Maritime : Centrer of trade upgrade (Prioritize the world port)
#Assimilation : State maintenance - - - (Multiple races at the same place)
#Nationalism : Dev cost in primary culture (Development only for our kind)
#Society : Stability Cost Modifier/ Monthly Reform Progress (Pillar of unity)
#propaganda : Yearly Legitimacy/Improve Relations Modifier (Voices of the Crown or the ring ? my precious)
#Imperialist ambition : Warscore Cost for Provinces/Core Creation Cost (Comander and Conquier)
#Imperialism : centralize state cost (big city of the empire)
#High Seas :Naval Maintenance Modifier/ Global Ship Repair
#Amphibious Ideas : Disembark Speed / Movment speed (Drilling on Morce march tactics)
#Magocratic : Magical study experience / adm advisor cost
#Monstruous : Administrative Efficiency (Beasts of Bureaucracy)
#Empire of Anbennar Ideas :Imperial authority (strengh to pass reform)
#Artificery :Rebel suppression efficiency ( Bravem)
#War Production : Artillery Cost, Recruitment time (Engines of Conquest)
#Shock : Shock damage / Cav power (Striking united)
#Fire :  fire Damage / Army tradition from battle
#Offensive : Siege ability / discipline ( capital military school of officer)
#Defensive : fort defence/ morale of armies
#Quality : Discipline / morale (Forged/train in the Core of the capital)
#Quantity :  MP / reinforce speed (Endless Legions of the crown)
#Strategic Ideas :Own territory dice roll bonus (defence of our borders)
#Serpentspine : centralize state cost (The best hold is a concentrated hold)
#Legionary ideas : Dev cost (Rising towers to reach the sun)
#General Staff Ideas : Leader Cost / Army Morale Recovery speed (Core of command)
#Standing Army :  Army morale / yearly proffessionalism
#Heroism : Mercenary Maintenance Modifier/State Governing Cost (Emissaries of the Throne)
#Conscription : Land force limit / Reinforce speed ( Draft for the Nation)
#Weapon Quality :  infantry fire/ artillery fire (Forged by the Crown)
#Forteress : Garrison size (Bigger forts)
#Militarism  : Dev cost + (Military workforce)

#############################################
# decentralism policies
#############################################
#Colonial Empire :Liberty Desire on Other Continent (Down the liberty desire only for colonies)
#Espionnage : Corruption / Institution spread (Track down the obscurantism sprayers)
#Diplomatic : Diplomatic anexion cost, diplo relation (come in my empire....)
#Influence : vassalisation acceptance (Enhance our demagogy to snatch new vasssals)
#Trade : Trade efficiency/ Ship trade power
#Exploration : minimum autonomy in territories
#Maritime : Trade range / naval force limit (A large empire need a large fleet)
#Assimilation : Max promoted culture ++ (Assimilation of everyone)
#Nationalism : Culture convert cost (Expulsion of everyone)
#Society : minimum autonomy in territories / monthly autonomy change
#propaganda : unrest - -
#Imperialist ambition : vassalisation acceptance
#Imperialism : Liberty desire in same continent (you are just a puppet stay still)
#High Seas :Naval combat bonus on owned coast / Naval force limit
#Amphibious Ideas : Disembark speed / Naval attrition (cover long distances of our empire)
#Magocratic : magical study experience / mage influence / liberty desire from subject (magical audit of the vassals)
#Monstruous : years of separatism - -
#Empire of Anbennar Ideas :reson to elect ( you are so good your highness)
#Artificery :Rebel suppression efficiency (George Anson policy)
#War Production : production efficiency / monthly autonomy change (weaponize militia)
#Shock : cavalry combat ability / cavalry flanking ability
#Fire :  Province warscore cost / Artillery combat ability
#Offensive : Recruitment time / land attrition
#Defensive : reinforce speed/ fort defence
#Quality : Discipline / morale (Forged/train in the Core of the capital)
#Quantity :  MP / reinforce speed (Endless Legions of the crown)
#Strategic Ideas :Capital dice roll bonus / Cost to moove the capital (Strategic repositioning in order to war)
#Serpentspine : Liberty desire of vassal (Verkal Ozovar experience)
#Legionary ideas : Liberty desire of vassal (Unifying Bulwar peacefuly)
#General Staff Ideas : Leader without upkeep + / Leader recruitment cost (Far off generals)
#Standing Army :  Army morale damage taken from reserves
#Heroism : Mercenary Manpower (pas beaucoup)/Governing Cost in Territories (Champions of the Far Regions)
#Conscription : Land force limit / Reinforce speed (Frontier army)
#Weapon Quality :  Infantry shock (Flat) / Cavalry shock (flat) (Charge into new territories)
#Forteress : Fort maintenance (Wall of china)
#Militarism  : Land force limit (Lige man)

#Colonial Empire : Colony devleopment boost (Experienced settlers enhance the new colonies)
#Espionnage : Siege ability / Fort defence (Stealing Forteress contruction plans)
#Diplomatic : Improve relation modifier / Diplomatic reputation (French Fancy gardens)
#Influence : num accepted cultures / Fort defence (Fortify the marches)
#Trade : Caravan power / Institution spread
#Exploration : Colony devleopment boost (Bigger Settlements in aelantir)
#Maritime : Ship cost / Construction speed (Development of major Harbors)
#Assimilation : Construction cost / Construction speed (More District for everyone)
#Nationalism : Dev cost in primary culture (Separated District from other races)
#Society : Dev cost modifier (Builder of nations)
#propaganda : Unrest - - (Over building watch towers)
#Imperialist ambition : Dev cost modifier (Building for prosperity)
#Imperialism : Prosperity growth (The benefit of prosperity)
#High Seas : global ship recruit speed /global ship repair (better ship facilities)
#Amphibious Ideas : global ship recruit speed /global ship repair (better ship facilities)
#Magocratic : Construction cost (Esoteric material building)
#Monstruous : Dev cost (Slave at work)
#Empire of Anbennar Ideas :Global building (Constructing even bigger tower)
#Artificery :Construction cost ( Gobline archiotecture)
#War Production : global_allowed_num_of_manufactories(Civil manufactures)
#Shock : Attrition for enemy (Dragon tooth deployment)
#Fire :  Attrition for enemy (Building Cannon tower)
#Offensive : Fort maintenance / Fire damage recived (Brace ourselves for the volley)
#Defensive : fort maintenace / shock damage recieve (Brace ourselves for the shock) 
#Quality : Building cost + / Good produced flat +0,25 (Better building technic)
#Quantity :  Building cost - - - (Made in Yanshen)
#Strategic Ideas :Construction speed /Rival fort maintenance / Fort defence ++  (Hide behind the walls)
#Serpentspine : Dev cost modifier (DIG DIG DIG DIG DIG DIG GID fuck i messed up)
#Legionary ideas : Construction cost / Fort defence / Garrison size
#General Staff Ideas : Gold inflation / gold_depletion_chance_modifier (Military guarding the golden mine)
#Standing Army :  Global proserity growth / Caravan power (Construct outpost on trading roads)
#Heroism : Build Cost/Global Prosperity Growth (Guardians of the Roads)
#Conscription : Global proserity growth / Build speed (make them work for the country)
#Weapon Quality :  Production efficiency / Trade efficiency (Infrastructure of quality (Lame name HAHA))
#Forteress : Fort defence +++ / Attrition / Max attrition (Vauban System)
#Militarism  : Dev cost + (Military workforce)

# Influence
#############################################
#imperialism :Can create client state
#Artificery :Papal influence ++
#War Production : Liberty desire / Rebel support efficiency (Lord of war)
#Shock : Cav/Inf Ratio (Combined army)
#Fire :  Improve relation/ libery desire from subject (Burning influence)
#Offensive : Liberty desire in subject (Threaten them to steal some of thier land rights)
#Defensive : morale damage taken to reserve (Vassal cannon fooder)
#Quality : Vassal income / Vassal force limit contribution (Vassal of quality)
#Quantity :  num accepted cultures ++ (More vassals possible)
#Strategic Ideas :Vassalisation acceptance
#Serpentspine : num accepted cultures + (An other slave state to deepen the holds)
#Legionary ideas : Vassal force limit contribution (Force recruitment from the overlord)
#General Staff Ideas : Leader without upkeep / Land leader cost (Recruiting Generals in vassalized territory)
#Standing Army :  Possible condotiery ++ (The prowess of our mens at arms)
#Heroism : Diplomatic Reputation/Unjustified Demands (Diplomatic Heroes)
#Conscription : Vassal force limit contribution (More vassal force for the field)
#Weapon Quality :  Production efficiency / Years of personnal union integration
#Forteress : Income from vassal / Garrison size
#Militarism  : Vassal force limit contribution / Infantry combat ability

    }

#############################################
# Maritime
#############################################
#High sea:Possible flagship +1
#Artificery :number_of_cannons_modifier minimum
#War Production : Ship durability (Naval industry for sturdier ships)
#Shock : Global naval engagement modifier
#Fire :  number_of_cannons_modifier minimum
#Offensive : Naval leader maneuver
#Defensive : naval_morale_damage_received 
#Quality : discipline for marines (Very technical spyglasses)
#Quantity :  Global naval engagement modifier (Overwhelm them, This is our sea!)
